Max functions are piecewise, not polynomial in T.

Candidate 45 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 46:
$T^{c_0}c_1|\epsilon|^{c_2} + c_3 e^{c_4\epsilon} + c_5 e^{c_6\epsilon} + c_7$

Setting c_0 = 1, c_2 = 3: $Tc_1\epsilon^3 + c_3 e^{c_4\epsilon} + c_5 e^{c_6\epsilon} + c_7$

This gives T·ε³. Setting c_4 = 0, c_6 = 0: $Tc_1\epsilon^3 + c_3 + c_5 + c_7$ = T·ε³ + constant.

Missing: ε³ and T terms. Can't get them.

What if c_0 ≠ 1? Then $T^{c_0}$ is not linear in T.

Candidate 46 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 47:
$Tc_0\epsilon + c_1\epsilon^2 + c_2 e^{c_3\epsilon} + c_4 e^{c_5/T} + c_6\text{Max}(0, c_7+|\epsilon|)^5$

T dependence: T·ε and $e^{c_5/T}$. No T·ε³.

Candidate 47 verdict: [NO MATCH]

T dependence through $T\log(c_1|\epsilon|+1)$, which is not T·ε³.
